2010 Magic: The Gathering World Championships: Top Extended Deck Lists
======================================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on December 12, 2010 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











Listed below are all lists from Day 3 at Worlds which recorded 13 or more points in the six rounds of Extended.

#####
